\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_translator_macedonian_abb15cd7014f193003152208f0a5f9672}\label{class_translator_macedonian_abb15cd7014f193003152208f0a5f9672}} 
\index{TranslatorMacedonian@{TranslatorMacedonian}!idLanguage@{idLanguage}}
\index{idLanguage@{idLanguage}!TranslatorMacedonian@{TranslatorMacedonian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{idLanguage()}{idLanguage()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} Translator\+Macedonian\+::id\+Language (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Used for identification of the language. The identification should not be translated. It should be replaced by the name of the language in English using lower-\/case characters only (e.\+g. \char`\"{}czech\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}japanese\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}russian\char`\"{}, etc.). It should be equal to the identification used in language.\+cpp. 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{class_translator_af1d1a225ccc757c51c6cecfeda886b93}{Translator}}.

Used for identification of the language. The identification should not be translated. It should be replaced by the name of the language in English using lower-\/case characters only (e.\+g. \char`\"{}czech\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}japanese\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}russian\char`\"{}, etc.). \end{DoxyCode}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_translator_macedonian_a256abae5c4aa6cb625159ab95fd9d539}\label{class_translator_macedonian_a256abae5c4aa6cb625159ab95fd9d539}} 
\index{TranslatorMacedonian@{TranslatorMacedonian}!latexLanguageSupportCommand@{latexLanguageSupportCommand}}
\index{latexLanguageSupportCommand@{latexLanguageSupportCommand}!TranslatorMacedonian@{TranslatorMacedonian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{latexLanguageSupportCommand()}{latexLanguageSupportCommand()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} Translator\+Macedonian\+::latex\+Language\+Support\+Command (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Used to get the La\+TeX command(s) for the language support. This method should return string with commands that switch La\+TeX to the desired language. For example 
\begin{DoxyPre}"{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)usepackage[german]\{babel\}\(\backslash\)n"{}
 \end{DoxyPre}
 or 
\begin{DoxyPre}"{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)usepackage\{polski\}\(\backslash\)n"{}
 "{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)usepackage[latin2]\{inputenc\}\(\backslash\)n"{}
 "{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)usepackage[T1]\{fontenc\}\(\backslash\)n"{}
 \end{DoxyPre}


The English La\+TeX does not use such commands. Because of this the empty string is returned in this implementation. 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{class_translator_aa2cff88fa1aa000c9f5efe2ac12c4448}{Translator}}.



Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__mk_8h_source_l00064}{64}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2translator__mk_8h_source}{translator\+\_\+mk.\+h}}.

Used to get the La\+TeX command(s) for the language support. This method should return string with commands that switch La\+TeX to the desired language. For example 
\begin{DoxyPre}"{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)usepackage[german]\{babel\}\(\backslash\)n"{}
 \end{DoxyPre}
 or 
\begin{DoxyPre}"{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)usepackage\{polski\}\(\backslash\)n"{}
 "{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)usepackage[latin2]\{inputenc\}\(\backslash\)n"{}
 "{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)usepackage[T1]\{fontenc\}\(\backslash\)n"{}
 \end{DoxyPre}


The English La\+TeX does not use such commands. Because of this the empty string is returned in this implementation. 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{class_translator_aa2cff88fa1aa000c9f5efe2ac12c4448}{Translator}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_translator_macedonian_a7daf5f1d4e735c35965e3b9600423532}\label{class_translator_macedonian_a7daf5f1d4e735c35965e3b9600423532}} 
\index{TranslatorMacedonian@{TranslatorMacedonian}!trSearchResults@{trSearchResults}}
\index{trSearchResults@{trSearchResults}!TranslatorMacedonian@{TranslatorMacedonian}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{trSearchResults()}{trSearchResults()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} Translator\+Macedonian\+::tr\+Search\+Results (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{num\+Documents }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This string is put just before listing the search results. The text can be different depending on the number of documents found. Inside the text you can put the special marker \$num to insert the number representing the actual number of search results. The {\itshape num\+Documents} parameter can be either 0, 1 or 2, where the value 2 represents 2 or more matches. HTML markup is allowed inside the returned string. 

Implements \mbox{\hyperlink{class_translator_aac55ca755f3f6bffc8baf2162bea7771}{Translator}}.

\DoxyCodeLine{00648                                    \textcolor{comment}{// (order is left to right)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00649 }
